<h1 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center has-large-font-size">She knows Islands &#8211; The European Islands Travel Blog</h1>



<div class="wp-block-group alignwide"><div class="wp-block-group__inner-container is-layout-constrained wp-block-group-is-layout-constrained">
<div class="wp-block-columns alignwide are-vertically-aligned-center has-background is-layout-flex wp-container-core-columns-is-layout-9d6595d7 wp-block-columns-is-layout-flex" style="background-color:#f2fafd">
<div class="wp-block-column is-vertically-aligned-center is-layout-flow wp-block-column-is-layout-flow" style="flex-basis:33.33%"><div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-full is-resized"><picture><source srcset="https://sheknowsislands.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/01/Linda-on-the-island-of-Malta.webp 936w,https://sheknowsislands.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/01/Linda-on-the-island-of-Malta-300x289.webp 300w,https://sheknowsislands.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/01/Linda-on-the-island-of-Malta-768x739.webp 768w" sizes="(max-width: 936px) 100vw, 936px" type="image/webp"><img src="https://sheknowsislands.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/01/Linda-on-the-island-of-Malta.jpg" height="901" width="936" srcset="https://sheknowsislands.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/01/Linda-on-the-island-of-Malta.jpg 936w, https://sheknowsislands.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/01/Linda-on-the-island-of-Malta-300x289.jpg 300w, https://sheknowsislands.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/01/Linda-on-the-island-of-Malta-768x739.jpg 768w" sizes="(max-width: 936px) 100vw, 936px" class="wp-image-134 sp-no-webp" alt="Linda taking a selfi in front of the rocky coastline of Malta, a european island." decoding="async" style="width:auto;height:300px"  > </picture></figure>
</div></div>



<div class="wp-block-column is-vertically-aligned-center is-layout-flow wp-block-column-is-layout-flow" style="flex-basis:66.66%">
<p class="has-medium-font-size">I&#8217;m Linda: a travel blogging expert, avid hiker, and island enthusiast. Particularly during the chilly German winters, I flee and spend my time exploring the sunny islands of Europe such as <a href="https://sheknowsislands.com/category/mallorca/" data-type="category" data-id="12">Mallorca</a>, <a href="https://sheknowsislands.com/malta/" data-type="page" data-id="753">Malta</a>, or <a href="https://sheknowsislands.com/sicily/" data-type="page" data-id="1005">Sicily</a>.</p>



<p>My goal is to make your island trips in Europe easier and more fun. I&#8217;ve got all the info you need to make sure your vacation is smooth and super enjoyable.</p>
</div>
</div>



<hr class="wp-block-separator has-alpha-channel-opacity"/>



<div style="height:30px" aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-spacer"></div>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center has-large-font-size">Start here: Choose your European Island</h2>



<div class="wp-block-columns is-layout-flex wp-container-core-columns-is-layout-9d6595d7 wp-block-columns-is-layout-flex">
<div class="wp-block-column is-layout-flow wp-block-column-is-layout-flow">
<h3 class="wp-block-heading"><a href="https://sheknowsislands.com/malta/" data-type="link" data-id="https://sheknowsislands.com/malta/">Chios</a></h3>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><a href="https://sheknowsislands.com/chios/"><picture><source srcset="https://sheknowsislands.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/Destination-Chios-scaled.webp 2560w,https://sheknowsislands.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/Destination-Chios-300x50.webp 300w,https://sheknowsislands.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/Destination-Chios-1024x171.webp 1024w,https://sheknowsislands.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/Destination-Chios-768x128.webp 768w,https://sheknowsislands.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/Destination-Chios-1536x256.webp 1536w,https://sheknowsislands.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/Destination-Chios-2048x341.webp 2048w" sizes="(max-width: 2560px) 100vw, 2560px" type="image/webp"><img src="https://sheknowsislands.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/Destination-Chios-scaled.jpg" height="427" width="2560" srcset="https://sheknowsislands.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/Destination-Chios-scaled.jpg 2560w, https://sheknowsislands.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/Destination-Chios-300x50.jpg 300w, https://sheknowsislands.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/Destination-Chios-1024x171.jpg 1024w, https://sheknowsislands.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/Destination-Chios-768x128.jpg 768w, https://sheknowsislands.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/Destination-Chios-1536x256.jpg 1536w, https://sheknowsislands.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/Destination-Chios-2048x341.jpg 2048w" sizes="(max-width: 2560px) 100vw, 2560px" class="wp-image-1333 sp-no-webp" alt="A banner featuring highlights of Chios, Greece, with three circular images showcasing Chios mastic tears, traditional windmills at sunset, and an aerial view of a lighthouse on a small islet, all against a serene blue background with the text &#039;CHIOS&#039; in bold white letters." decoding="async"  > </picture></a></figure>
